It is a visual template pre-formatted with the nine blocks of a business model.\r\nFormal descriptions of the business become the building blocks for its activities. Many different business conceptualizations exist; Osterwalder's work and thesis propose a single reference model based on the similarities of a wide range of business model conceptualizations. With his business model design template, an enterprise can easily describe their business model.\r\nPartner Network: The business alliances which complement other aspects of the business model.\r\nKey Activities: The activities necessary to execute a company's business model.\r\nKey Resources: The resources that are necessary to create value for the customer.\r\nValue Proposition:The products and services a business offers. This includes the company's marketing and  distribution strategy.\r\nCustomer Relationship: The links a company establishes between itself and its different customer segments. The process of managing customer relationships is referred to as customer relationship management.\r\nCost Structure: The monetary consequences of the means employed in the business model.\r\nRevenue Streams: The way a company makes money through a variety of revenue flows. A company's income.\r\nThis App helps you generate a business model using the canvas of nine blocks.
